connection coefficients / 2nd kind Christoffel: ${{{{ \Gamma}^{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{r}}} = {-{\frac{1}{{{2}} {{{r}^{({\frac{3}{2}})}}}}}}$; ${{{{ \Gamma}^{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{\theta}}} = {-{\sqrt r}}$; ${{{{ \Gamma}^{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{\theta}}} = {\frac{1}{{{2}} {{{r}^{({\frac{3}{2}})}}}}}$; ${{{{ \Gamma}^{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{r}}} = {\frac{1}{{r}^{({\frac{3}{2}})}}}$

connection coefficients squared: ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{r}}} = {\frac{1}{{{4}} {{{r}^{3}}}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{\theta}}} = {-{\frac{1}{r}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{\theta}}} = {\frac{1}{{{2}} {{r}}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{r}}} = {-{\frac{1}{{{2}} {{r}}}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{\theta}}} = {\frac{1}{{{2}} {{{r}^{3}}}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{r}}} = {-{\frac{1}{{{2}} {{{r}^{3}}}}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{r}}}_{\bar{r}}} = {\frac{1}{{{4}} {{{r}^{3}}}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{\theta}}}_{\bar{\theta}}} = {-{\frac{1}{r}}}$

cylindrical surface, anholonomic, normalized

coordinates: $\bar{\phi}$ $\bar{z}$
base coords: $\phi$ $z$
embedding: $x$ $y$ $z$
flat metric:
${{{ \eta}_x}_x} = {1}$; ${{{ \eta}_y}_y} = {1}$; ${{{ \eta}_z}_z} = {1}$

chart:
${{ u}^x} = {{{r}} {{cos\left( \phi\right)}}}$; ${{ u}^y} = {{{r}} {{sin\left( \phi\right)}}}$; ${{ u}^z} = {z}$

basis:
${{{ e}_u}^I} = {{{ u}^I}_{,u}}$
${{{ e}_{\bar{\phi}}}^x} = {-{sin\left( \phi\right)}}$; ${{{ e}_{\bar{\phi}}}^y} = {cos\left( \phi\right)}$; ${{{ e}_{\bar{z}}}^z} = {\frac{1}{r}}$
${{{ e}^{\bar{\phi}}}_x} = {{\frac{1}{r}}{({-{sin\left( \phi\right)}})}}$; ${{{ e}^{\bar{\phi}}}_y} = {{\frac{1}{r}}{({cos\left( \phi\right)})}}$; ${{{ e}^{\bar{z}}}_z} = {1}$
${{{{{ e}_u}^I}} {{{{ e}^v}_I}}} = {\overset{u\downarrow v\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} \frac{1}{r} & 0 \\ 0 & \frac{1}{r}\end{matrix}\right]}}$
${{{{{ e}_u}^I}} {{{{ e}^u}_J}}} = {\overset{I\downarrow J\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {\frac{1}{r}}{({{1} - {{cos\left( \phi\right)}^{2}}})} & {\frac{1}{r}}{({-{{{sin\left( \phi\right)}} {{cos\left( \phi\right)}}}})} & 0 \\ {\frac{1}{r}}{({-{{{cos\left( \phi\right)}} {{sin\left( \phi\right)}}}})} & {\frac{1}{r}}{({{cos\left( \phi\right)}^{2}})} & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & \frac{1}{r}\end{matrix}\right]}}$

connection coefficients squared: ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^t}_t}_r}_r} = {\frac{{R}^{2}}{{{{r}^{2}}} {{({{{{{4}} {{{r}^{2}}}} - {{{8}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{4}} {{{R}^{2}}}}})}}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^r}_r}_r}_r} = {\frac{{{{R}^{2}}} {{({{{{R}^{2}} - {{{2}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{r}^{2}}})}}}{{{{r}^{2}}} {{({{{{{4}} {{{r}^{4}}}} - {{{16}} {{r}} {{{R}^{3}}}}} + {{{{24}} {{{R}^{2}}} {{{r}^{2}}}} - {{{16}} {{R}} {{{r}^{3}}}}} + {{{4}} {{{R}^{4}}}}})}}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\theta}}_{\theta}}_r}_r} = {\frac{1}{{r}^{2}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\phi}}_{\phi}}_r}_r} = {\frac{1}{{r}^{2}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\phi}}_{\phi}}_r}_{\theta}} = {\frac{cos\left( \theta\right)}{{{r}} {{sin\left( \theta\right)}}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\phi}}_{\phi}}_{\theta}}_r} = {\frac{cos\left( \theta\right)}{{{sin\left( \theta\right)}} {{r}}}}$; ${{{{{ {(\Gamma^2)}}^{\phi}}_{\phi}}_{\theta}}_{\theta}} = {\frac{{cos\left( \theta\right)}^{2}}{{1} - {{cos\left( \theta\right)}^{2}}}}$
Riemann curvature, $\sharp\flat\flat\flat$: ${{{{{ R}^{\phi}}_{\phi}}_r}_{\theta}} = {\frac{-{cos\left( \theta\right)}}{{{sin\left( \theta\right)}} {{r}}}}$; ${{{{{ R}^{\phi}}_{\phi}}_{\theta}}_r} = {\frac{cos\left( \theta\right)}{{{sin\left( \theta\right)}} {{r}}}}$
Riemann curvature, $\sharp\sharp\flat\flat$: ${{{{{ R}^{\phi}}^{\phi}}_r}_{\theta}} = {\frac{cos\left( \theta\right)}{{{{r}^{3}}} {{sin\left( \theta\right)}} {{({{-{1}} + {{cos\left( \theta\right)}^{2}}})}}}}$; ${{{{{ R}^{\phi}}^{\phi}}_{\theta}}_r} = {\frac{cos\left( \theta\right)}{-{{{{r}^{3}}} {{sin\left( \theta\right)}} {{({{-{1}} + {{cos\left( \theta\right)}^{2}}})}}}}}$
Ricci curvature, $\sharp\flat$: ${{{ R}^a}_b} = {0}$
Gaussian curvature: $0$
Einstein $\sharp\flat$ / trace-reversed Ricci curvature: ${{{ G}^a}_b} = {0}$
divergence: ${{{{ A}^i}_{,i}} + {{{{{{ \Gamma}^i}_i}_j}} {{{ A}^j}}}} = {{{{{A^{r}}}} \cdot {{{R}^{2}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{r}} {{{r}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{r}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{r}} {{{R}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{-4}} {{R}} {{r}} {{{\partial {A^{\phi}}}\over{\partial\phi}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{-4}} {{R}} {{r}} {{{\partial {A^{\theta}}}\over{\partial\theta}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{-4}} {{R}} {{r}} {{{\partial {A^{r}}}\over{\partial r}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{-4}} {{R}} {{r}} {{{\partial {A^{t}}}\over{\partial t}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{-1}} {{R}} {{{A^{r}}}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}} {{{\partial {A^{\phi}}}\over{\partial\phi}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}} {{{\partial {A^{\theta}}}\over{\partial\theta}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}} {{{\partial {A^{r}}}\over{\partial r}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}} {{{\partial {A^{t}}}\over{\partial t}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}} {{{\partial {A^{\phi}}}\over{\partial\phi}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}} {{{\partial {A^{\theta}}}\over{\partial\theta}}} {{\frac{1}{{{{{2}} {{{R}^{2}}}} - {{{4}} {{R}} {{r}}}} + {{{2}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}}}$
geodesic:
${\overset{a\downarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} \ddot{t} \\ \ddot{r} \\ \ddot{\theta} \\ \ddot{\phi}\end{matrix}\right]}} = {\overset{a\downarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {{-1}} {{R}} {{\dot{r}}} \cdot {{\dot{t}}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{{{{-2}} {{r}} {{R}}} + {{{2}} {{r}} {{r}}}}}} \\ {{{-1}} {{R}} {{{\dot{r}}^{2}}} {{R}} {{\frac{1}{{{{2}} {{r}} {{{R}^{2}}}} + {{{-4}} {{r}} {{R}} {{r}}} + {{{2}} {{r}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} + {{{R}} {{{\dot{r}}^{2}}} {{r}} {{\frac{1}{{{{2}} {{r}} {{{R}^{2}}}} + {{{-4}} {{r}} {{R}} {{r}}} + {{{2}} {{r}} {{{r}^{2}}}}}}}} \\ {{-1}} {{\dot{r}}} \cdot {{\dot{\theta}}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{r}}} \\ {{{-1}} {{\dot{\phi}}} \cdot {{\dot{r}}} \cdot {{sin\left( \theta\right)}} {{\frac{1}{sin\left( \theta\right)}}} {{\frac{1}{r}}}} + {{{-1}} {{\dot{\phi}}} \cdot {{r}} {{\dot{\theta}}} \cdot {{cos\left( \theta\right)}} {{\frac{1}{sin\left( \theta\right)}}} {{\frac{1}{r}}}}\end{matrix}\right]}}$
